%%\tagged{Cat@One, Cat@Two, Cat@Three, Cat@Four, Cat@Five, Ans@MultiAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Product_Rule, Sub@Multi_Deriv}{

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{16 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{4}{x} - 4 \, \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{4}{x} - \frac{16 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{20}{x^{2}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{4}{x^{2}} + \frac{32 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{56}{x^{3}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\cos\left(x\right)^{2} - 4 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-2 \, \cos\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-2 \, \cos\left(x\right)^{2} + 2 \, \sin\left(x\right)^{2} + 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={x - \frac{1}{x} - \frac{4}{x^{2}} + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{1}{x^{2}} + \frac{8}{x^{3}} + 1}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{2}{x^{3}} - \frac{24}{x^{4}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 15 \, x^{4} + 15 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{25 \, x^{4} \cos\left(x\right) + 100 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) + 60 \, x^{3} + 15 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-25 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 200 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 300 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 180 \, x^{2} - 15 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={4 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - 2 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 2 \, \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-4 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{2}{x} + 2 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - \frac{8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{2}{x^{2}} + 2 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 6 \, \sqrt{x} - 6 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{9 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - \frac{3}{\sqrt{x}} - 6 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{3}{2 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, x^{2} + \frac{16}{x^{2}} + 32}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{32 \, x - \frac{32}{x^{3}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{96}{x^{4}} + 32}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-\frac{6}{x} - \frac{6}{x^{2}} + \frac{9}{x^{3}} + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{6}{x^{2}} + \frac{12}{x^{3}} - \frac{27}{x^{4}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{12}{x^{3}} - \frac{36}{x^{4}} + \frac{108}{x^{5}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{15}{x} - 15 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{15}{x^{2}} - 15 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{50 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{50 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{30}{x^{3}} + 15 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{4}{x} + \frac{4}{x^{2}} + \frac{1}{x^{3}} + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{4}{x^{2}} - \frac{8}{x^{3}} - \frac{3}{x^{4}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{8}{x^{3}} + \frac{24}{x^{4}} + \frac{12}{x^{5}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={4 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + 4 \, \log\left(x\right) + 4 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{4 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) + \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{4}{x} + 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{8 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{4}{x^{2}} - 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\begin{problem}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{2}{x^{2}} - \frac{4}{x^{3}} - 4}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{4}{x^{3}} + \frac{12}{x^{4}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={4 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 4 \, x^{4} + 4 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{4 \, x^{4} \cos\left(x\right) + 16 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) + 16 \, x^{3} + 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 32 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 48 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 48 \, x^{2} - 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={x^{3} e^{x} - 3 \, x^{3} - 3 \, e^{x} + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{x^{3} e^{x} + 3 \, x^{2} e^{x} - 9 \, x^{2} - 3 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{x^{3} e^{x} + 6 \, x^{2} e^{x} + 6 \, x e^{x} - 18 \, x - 3 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{4}{x^{3}} - 4 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{12 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} + \frac{12}{x^{4}} - 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{24 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} + \frac{48 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{5}} - \frac{48}{x^{5}} + 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\begin{problem}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{32 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{8}{x^{3}} + 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{64 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{96 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{24}{x^{4}} + 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\sqrt{x} \log\left(x\right) + \sqrt{x} + \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{\log\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{3}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{1}{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{\log\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{1}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{1}{x^{2}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, x^{2} \log\left(x\right) + 4 \, x^{2} + 4 \, \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{32 \, x \log\left(x\right) + 24 \, x + \frac{4}{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{4}{x^{2}} + 32 \, \log\left(x\right) + 56}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{3 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} - \frac{6}{x^{4}} + 2 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{6 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{12 \, e^{x}}{x^{5}} + \frac{24}{x^{5}} + 2 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) + 24 \, x^{2} \cos\left(x\right) + 24 \, x \sin\left(x\right) - 48 \, x + 8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{27 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{18}{x^{4}} - 6 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{54 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{108 \, e^{x}}{x^{5}} - \frac{72}{x^{5}} - 6 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{3}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 12 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 3 \, x^{2} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{x^{2} \cos\left(x\right) + 2 \, x \sin\left(x\right) + 6 \, x + 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 4 \, x \cos\left(x\right) - \sin\left(x\right) + 6}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, e^{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 5 \, e^{x} - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{25 \, \cos\left(x\right) e^{x} + 25 \, e^{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 5 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 5 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{50 \, \cos\left(x\right) e^{x} - 5 \, e^{x} + 5 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{16}{x} + 16 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{16}{x^{2}} - 16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{32 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{32 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{32}{x^{3}} - 16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={5 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 4 \, x - 10 \, \sqrt{x} + 8}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{15}{2} \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 4}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{15}{4 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{5}{2 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-3 \, x^{2} + 9 \, x - \frac{3}{x} + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-6 \, x + \frac{3}{x^{2}} + 9}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{6}{x^{3}} - 6}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{16 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{4}{x^{3}} + 4 \, e^{x} + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{16 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{48 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} - \frac{12}{x^{4}} + 4 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{16 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{96 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{192 \, e^{x}}{x^{5}} + \frac{48}{x^{5}} + 4 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{50 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} + \frac{50 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{20}{x^{3}} - 10 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + 20 \, \sqrt{x} + 20 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-25 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{10}{\sqrt{x}} - 20 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-25 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) - \frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{5}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - 20 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{25 \, \sqrt{x} e^{x} + \frac{25 \, e^{x}}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{25 \, e^{x}}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{15}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 15 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{32 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{32 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{40}{x^{3}} - 20 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{12}{x} + 12 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{12}{x^{2}} + 12 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{18 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{18 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{24}{x^{3}} - 12 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\begin{problem}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{25 \, x^{4} \cos\left(x\right) + 100 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) + 20 \, x^{3} + 5 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-25 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 200 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 300 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 60 \, x^{2} - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + 3 \, \sqrt{x} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{9 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{3}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{3}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - 3 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{10}{x^{3}} - \frac{45}{x^{4}} - 5}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{30}{x^{4}} + \frac{180}{x^{5}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f'(x)=\answer{x \cos\left(x\right) + 5 \, \cos\left(x\right) + \sin\left(x\right) + 1}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-x \sin\left(x\right) + 2 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{4 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{6 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{30}{x^{4}} + 5 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 8 \, \sqrt{x} - 8 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{16 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}} - 8 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{2}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{5}{x^{3}} + 5 \, e^{x} + 25}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{3 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} - \frac{15}{x^{4}} + 5 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{6 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{12 \, e^{x}}{x^{5}} + \frac{60}{x^{5}} + 5 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, x^{3} \log\left(x\right) - 20 \, x^{3} - 20 \, \log\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{75 \, x^{2} \log\left(x\right) - 35 \, x^{2} - \frac{20}{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{150 \, x \log\left(x\right) + 5 \, x + \frac{20}{x^{2}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} \log\left(x\right) + 6 \, \sqrt{x} + 6 \, \log\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, \log\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{12}{\sqrt{x}} + \frac{6}{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{9 \, \log\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{3}{2 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{6}{x^{2}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\[f'(x)=\answer{175 \, x^{6} + 100 \, x^{3} + 75 \, x^{2}}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) + 4 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 4 \, \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-16 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{4}{x} - 4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - \frac{32 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{4}{x^{2}} - 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)^{2} - 16 \, \sin\left(x\right)^{2} - 20 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 20 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-64 \, \cos\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + 20 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 20 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={4 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + 2 \, e^{x} + 2 \, \log\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{4 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{4 \, e^{x}}{x} + \frac{2}{x} + 2 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{4 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{8 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{4 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{2}{x^{2}} + 2 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{x^{2} e^{x} + 2 \, x e^{x} - 2 \, x - e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{x^{2} e^{x} + 4 \, x e^{x} + e^{x} - 2}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f'(x)=\answer{2 \, \cos\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) - 4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\end{problem}}%}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{1}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) - \frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{1}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) - 3 \, x^{4} - 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{x^{4} \cos\left(x\right) + 4 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) - 12 \, x^{3} - 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 8 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 12 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) - 36 \, x^{2} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - 8 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 8 \, \log\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-16 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{8}{x} + 8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - \frac{32 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{8}{x^{2}} + 8 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-5 \, x \cos\left(x\right) + 15 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right) - 2}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{5 \, x \sin\left(x\right) - 10 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 15 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-8 \, x^{2} + 16 \, x - \frac{8}{x} + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-16 \, x + \frac{8}{x^{2}} + 16}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16}{x^{3}} - 16}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-6 \, x^{2} + \frac{9}{x} - \frac{6}{x^{3}} + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-12 \, x - \frac{9}{x^{2}} + \frac{18}{x^{4}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{18}{x^{3}} - \frac{72}{x^{5}} - 12}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{8}{x} - \frac{48 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{8}{x^{4}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{8}{x^{2}} + \frac{192 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{5}} - \frac{16}{x^{5}}}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + 10 \, e^{x} + 10 \, \log\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{25 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x} + \frac{10}{x} + 10 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{25 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{50 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{10}{x^{2}} + 10 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{3}{x^{2}} - 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{2 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{6}{x^{3}} - 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{18}{x^{4}} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + 12 \, \sqrt{x} + 12 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{6}{\sqrt{x}} - 12 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-9 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) - \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{3}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - 12 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-x^{4} \cos\left(x\right) - 8 \, x^{3} \sin\left(x\right) + 12 \, x^{2} \cos\left(x\right) + 24 \, x^{2} - 2 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{10}{x^{2}} - 10 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 25}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{20}{x^{3}} - 10 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{24 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{60}{x^{4}} + 10 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 10 \, \sqrt{x} - 10 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{25 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - \frac{5}{\sqrt{x}} - 10 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-25 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{5}{2 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 10 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{64 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{96 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} + \frac{72}{x^{4}} - 12 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-9 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 72 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 108 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 180 \, x^{2} - 15 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{9 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{15}{x^{2}} + 15 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{9 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{18 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} + \frac{18 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{30}{x^{3}} + 15 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{4 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{4}{x^{2}} - 4 \, \log\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{4}{x} - \frac{8 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{12}{x^{3}}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{4}{x^{2}} + \frac{24 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{44}{x^{4}}}\]

\[f'(x)=\answer{15 \, x^{4} - 60 \, x^{3} + 4}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{60 \, x^{3} - 180 \, x^{2}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-32 \, e^{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 20 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 20 \, e^{x}}\]

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{4 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{4 \, e^{x}}{x} + \frac{8}{x} + 8 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{4 \, e^{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{8 \, e^{x}}{x} - \frac{4 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{8}{x^{2}} + 8 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={25 \, x^{6} + 50 \, x^{3} + 25}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{150 \, x^{5} + 150 \, x^{2}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{750 \, x^{4} + 300 \, x}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{10}{x^{2}} - 10 \, e^{x} + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{50 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{20}{x^{3}} - 10 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{25 \, e^{x}}{x^{2}} - \frac{100 \, e^{x}}{x^{3}} + \frac{150 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} - \frac{60}{x^{4}} - 10 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{1}{x^{3}} - e^{x} + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{3 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{3}{x^{4}} - e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{e^{x}}{x^{3}} - \frac{6 \, e^{x}}{x^{4}} + \frac{12 \, e^{x}}{x^{5}} - \frac{12}{x^{5}} - e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-5 \, x \cos\left(x\right) + 2 \, x - 10 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{5 \, x \sin\left(x\right) - 5 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 10 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 2}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{5 \, x \cos\left(x\right) + 10 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 10 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) - 6 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{16 \, x^{4} e^{x} + 128 \, x^{3} e^{x} + 192 \, x^{2} e^{x} + 144 \, x^{2} + 12 \, e^{x}}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} e^{x} + 15 \, \sqrt{x} + 15 \, e^{x} + 25}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{9 \, \sqrt{x} e^{x} + \frac{9 \, e^{x}}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{15}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} + 15 \, e^{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{9 \, \sqrt{x} e^{x} + \frac{9 \, e^{x}}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{9 \, e^{x}}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{15}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 15 \, e^{x}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={4 \, \log\left(x\right)^{2} + 20 \, \log\left(x\right) + 25}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{8 \, \frac{1}{x} \log\left(x\right) + \frac{20}{x}}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{\frac{8}{x}}{x} - \frac{8 \, \log\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{20}{x^{2}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{9 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - \frac{3}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-9 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{9 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{9 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{3}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16}{x} - 16 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{16}{x^{2}} + 16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{32 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{32 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{32}{x^{3}} + 16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) - 8 \, \log\left(x\right) - 8 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{16 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{8}{x} - 8 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{32 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{16 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{8}{x^{2}} + 8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{\frac{15}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{27}{4 \, x^{\frac{5}{2}}} - \frac{30}{x^{3}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, x^{4} \sin\left(x\right) + 32 \, x^{3} \cos\left(x\right) + 48 \, x^{2} \sin\left(x\right) + 72 \, x^{2} - 6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{50 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{50 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{20}{x^{3}} + 10 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\latexProblemContent{

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - \frac{2 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{5}{x^{2}} + 5 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} + \frac{30}{x^{4}} - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) - 3 \, \sqrt{x} - 3 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - \frac{3}{2 \, \sqrt{x}} - 3 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{\sin\left(x\right)}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + \frac{3}{4 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} + 3 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-3 \, x \cos\left(x\right) - 4 \, x - 15 \, \cos\left(x\right) - 20}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{3 \, x \sin\left(x\right) - 3 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 15 \, \sin\left(x\right) - 4}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{3 \, x \cos\left(x\right) + 15 \, \cos\left(x\right) + 6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={-3 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}} + 4 \, x - 12 \, \sqrt{x} + 16}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-\frac{9}{2} \, \sqrt{x} - \frac{6}{\sqrt{x}} + 4}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{9}{4 \, \sqrt{x}} + \frac{3}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}}}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} + \frac{6}{x^{3}} + 6 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 9}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{4 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{12 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} - \frac{18}{x^{4}} + 6 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{24 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{4}} + \frac{48 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{5}} + \frac{72}{x^{5}} - 6 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={\frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{5}{x} - 5 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 1}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{\frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{5}{x^{2}} - 5 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-\frac{25 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{50 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} + \frac{50 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{3}} - \frac{10}{x^{3}} + 5 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Compute the first and second derivatives for the function\\ $f(x)={16 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + 8 \, \sqrt{x} + 8 \, \sin\left(x\right) + 4}$.\\

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{16 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) + \frac{8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} + \frac{4}{\sqrt{x}} + 8 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-16 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{16 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{2}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - 8 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}

\input{2311-Compute-Derivative-0039.HELP.tex}

\[f'(x)=\answer{-25 \, \log\left(x\right) \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x} + \frac{10}{x} - 10 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-25 \, \cos\left(x\right) \log\left(x\right) - \frac{50 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{x} - \frac{25 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{x^{2}} - \frac{10}{x^{2}} - 10 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\]

\[f'(x)=\answer{-4 \, \sqrt{x} \sin\left(x\right) + \frac{2 \, \cos\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{x}} - 2 \, \sin\left(x\right)}\]

\[f''(x)=\answer{-4 \, \sqrt{x} \cos\left(x\right) - \frac{4 \, \sin\left(x\right)}{\sqrt{x}} - \frac{\cos\left(x\right)}{x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - \frac{1}{2 \, x^{\frac{3}{2}}} - 2 \, \cos\left(x\right)}\] 
\end{problem}}%}
